                                            <span class="delivery-card__desc">Ship directly to buyer</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>

                                <label class="delivery-card">
                                    <input type="checkbox"
                                           name="AllowHalfway"
                                           value="true"
                                           class="delivery-input"
                                           id="optMeetup" />
                                    <div class="delivery-card__body">
                                        <div class="delivery-card__check">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none" width="10" height="10">
                                                <path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" stroke-width="1.8" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <span class="delivery-card__icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="20" height="20">
                                                <circle cx="10" cy="10" r="7.5" />
                                                <path d="M10 5V10L13 13" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                                <circle cx="10" cy="10" r="2" fill="currentColor" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </span>
                                        <div>
                                            <span class="delivery-card__title">Pickup Halfway</span>
                                            <span class="delivery-card__desc">Meet at agreed spot</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>

                                <label class="delivery-card">
                                    <input type="checkbox"
                                           name="AllowPickup"
                                           value="true"
                                           class="delivery-input"
                                           id="optPickup" />
                                    <div class="delivery-card__body">
                                        <div class="delivery-card__check">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none" width="10" height="10">
                                                <path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" stroke-width="1.8" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <span class="delivery-card__icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="20" height="20">
                                                <path d="M3 9.5L10 3.5L17 9.5V16.5H3V9.5Z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                                <rect x="8" y="11" width="4" height="5.5" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </span>
                                        <div>
                                            <span class="delivery-card__title">Pickup</span>
                                            <span class="delivery-card__desc">Buyer comes to you</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>
                            </div>
                            <span class="fulfillment-err" id="fulfillmentError"></span>
                            <div class="progressive-field__actions">
                                <button type="button" class="btn btn--primary btn--continue" data-next="stealable">
                                    Continue
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12">
                                        <path d="M7.5 5L12.5 10L7.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <!-- Field 8: Stealable -->
                    <div class="progressive-field progressive-field--locked" data-field="stealable" id="fieldStealable">
                        <div class="progressive-field__header">
                            <span class="progressive-field__icon">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="18" height="18">
                                    <path d="M10 2.5L12 7L17 7.5L13 10.5L14 15.5L10 13L6 15.5L7 10.5L3 7.5L8 7L10 2.5Z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                </svg>
                            </span>
                            <div>
                                <h3 class="progressive-field__title">Make it Stealable?</h3>
                                <p class="progressive-field__hint">Sell faster with a limited-time discount (optional)</p>
                            </div>
                            <span class="progressive-field__status">🔒</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="progressive-field__body" style="display: none;">
                            <div class="stealable-card">
                                <label class="stealable-toggle-row" for="stealableToggle">
                                    <div class="stealable-toggle-row__left">
                                        <span class="stealable-icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="18" height="18">
                                                <path d="M10 2.5L12 7L17 7.5L13 10.5L14 15.5L10 13L6 15.5L7 10.5L3 7.5L8 7L10 2.5Z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </span>
                                        <div>
                                            <span class="stealable-toggle-row__title">Make this Stealable</span>
                                            <span class="stealable-toggle-row__desc">Buyers can claim it instantly at a discounted price</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="toggle-switch">
                                        <input type="checkbox"
                                               name="IsStealable"
                                               value="true"
                                               id="stealableToggle" />
                                        <span class="toggle-switch__track"></span>
                                    </div>
                                </label>

                                <div class="steal-duration" id="stealDurationPanel">
                                    <label class="field__label" for="stealDurationSelect">Steal window duration</label>
                                    <div class="select-wrap">
                                        <select name="StealDurationHours"
                                                class="field__select field__select--sm"
                                                id="stealDurationSelect">
                                            <option value="">Select duration</option>
                                            @foreach (var dur in ItemCreateViewModel.StealDurations)
                                            {
                                                <option value="@dur">@dur hours</option>
                                            }
                                        </select>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="progressive-field__actions">
                                <button type="button" class="btn btn--ghost btn--skip" data-next="summary">Skip</button>
                                <button type="button" class="btn btn--primary btn--continue" data-next="summary">
                                    Complete
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12">
                                        <path d="M5 10l5 5 5-5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <!-- UNIFIED SUMMARY CARD (shown after all fields complete) -->
                    <div class="listing-summary" id="listingSummary" style="display: none;">
                        <div class="summary-card">
                            <div class="summary-card__header">
                                <div class="summary-card__check">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" width="20" height="20">
                                        <path d="M20 6L9 17l-5-5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <h3 class="summary-card__title">Listing Preview</h3>
                                <span class="summary-card__hint">Click any row to edit</span>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 1: Title & Price -->
                            <div class="summary-row summary-row--main" data-edit-field="title">
                                <div class="summary-row__left">
                                    <span class="summary-label">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                            <path d="M2 4L5 2L13 10L10 12L2 4Z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Title
                                    </span>
                                    <span class="summary-value summary-value--title" id="summaryTitle">—</span>
                                </div>
                                <div class="summary-row__right" data-edit-field="price">
                                    <span class="summary-label">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                            <circle cx="8" cy="8" r="6" />
                                            <path d="M6 6C6 5.5 7 5 8 5C9 5 10 5.5 10 6C10 7 8.5 7.5 8 9" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Price
                                    </span>
                                    <span class="summary-value summary-value--price" id="summaryPrice">—</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 2: Category & Condition & Size -->
                            <div class="summary-row summary-row--meta">
                                <div class="summary-item" data-edit-field="category">
                                    <span class="summary-label">Category</span>
                                    <span class="summary-value" id="summaryCategory">—</span>
                                </div>
                                <div class="summary-item" data-edit-field="condition">
                                    <span class="summary-label">Condition</span>
                                    <span class="summary-value" id="summaryCondition">—</span>
                                </div>
                                <div class="summary-item" data-edit-field="size">
                                    <span class="summary-label">Size</span>
                                    <span class="summary-value" id="summarySize">—</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 3: Delivery Options -->
                            <div class="summary-row" data-edit-field="delivery">
                                <span class="summary-label">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                        <rect x="1.5" y="7.5" width="13" height="5.5" rx="1" />
                                        <circle cx="5" cy="13" r="1" />
                                        <circle cx="11" cy="13" r="1" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Delivery
                                </span>
                                <span class="summary-value" id="summaryDelivery">—</span>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 4: Stealable Status -->
                            <div class="summary-row" data-edit-field="stealable">
                                <span class="summary-label">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                        <path d="M8 1.5L9.5 5.5L14 6L10.5 8.5L11.5 13L8 10.5L4.5 13L5.5 8.5L2 6L6.5 5.5L8 1.5Z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Listing Type
                                </span>
                                <span class="summary-value" id="summaryStealable">—</span>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 5: Description -->
                            <div class="summary-row summary-row--description" data-edit-field="description">
                                <span class="summary-label">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                        <rect x="1.5" y="2.5" width="13" height="11" rx="1" />
                                        <path d="M4.5 6H11.5" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                        <path d="M4.5 8.5H9.5" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Description
                                </span>
                                <span class="summary-value summary-value--desc" id="summaryDescription">—</span>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Actions -->
                            <div class="summary-card__actions">
                                <button type="submit" class="btn btn--primary btn--publish" id="submitBtn">
                                    <span>Publish Listing</span>
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="15" height="15">
                                        <path d="M3.5 2.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v14.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.392l1.657-.348a6.449 6.449 0 014.271.572 8.973 8.973 0 003.965.972 6.7 6.7 0 002.341-.428 2.25 2.25 0 001.266-2.117V3.75a.75.75 0 00-1.125-.649 5.2 5.2 0 01-2.482.66c-1.788 0-3.318-.506-4.507-1.2a6.407 6.407 0 00-3.686-.956L3.5 2.75z" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <!-- Footer -->
                    <div class="create-footer">
                        <a asp-action="Index" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                        <span class="footer-hint" id="footerHint">Complete all fields to publish</span>
                    </div>

                </main>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';

                // =========================================================
                // PROGRESSIVE FIELD UNLOCKING WITH UNIFIED SUMMARY CARD
                // =========================================================
        
                const fields = [
                    { id: 'title', element: document.getElementById('fieldTitle'), validate: validateTitle },
                    { id: 'price', element: document.getElementById('fieldPrice'), validate: validatePrice },
                    { id: 'category', element: document.getElementById('fieldCategory'), validate: validateCategory },
                    { id: 'condition', element: document.getElementById('fieldCondition'), validate: validateCondition },
                    { id: 'size', element: document.getElementById('fieldSize'), validate: validateSize, optional: true },
                    { id: 'description', element: document.getElementById('fieldDescription'), validate: validateDescription },
                    { id: 'delivery', element: document.getElementById('fieldDelivery'), validate: validateDelivery },
                    { id: 'stealable', element: document.getElementById('fieldStealable'), validate: validateStealable, optional: true }
                ];

                let completedFields = new Set(['title']);
                let allFieldsCompleted = false;
                const progressFill = document.getElementById('progressiveFill');
                const progressText = document.getElementById('progressText');
                const listingSummary = document.getElementById('listingSummary');
                const footerHint = document.getElementById('footerHint');

                const priceInput = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                if (priceInput && priceInput.value === '0') {
                    priceInput.value = '';
                }

                // Validation functions
                function validateTitle() {
                    const title = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                    return title && title.value.trim().length > 0;
                }

                function validatePrice() {
                    const price = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                    return price && price.value && price.value.trim() !== '' && parseFloat(price.value) > 0;
                }

                function validateCategory() {
                    const category = document.getElementById('categoryHidden');
                    return category && category.value !== '';
                }

                function validateCondition() {
                    const condition = document.getElementById('conditionHidden');
                    return condition && condition.value !== '';
                }

                function validateSize() {
                    return true;
                }

                function validateDescription() {
                    const desc = document.getElementById('descInput');
                    return desc && desc.value.trim().length > 0;
                }

                function validateDelivery() {
                    const optDelivery = document.getElementById('optDelivery');
                    const optMeetup = document.getElementById('optMeetup');
                    const optPickup = document.getElementById('optPickup');
                    return (optDelivery && optDelivery.checked) ||
                           (optMeetup && optMeetup.checked) ||
                           (optPickup && optPickup.checked);
                }

                function validateStealable() {
                    const stealableToggle = document.getElementById('stealableToggle');
                    const stealDurationSelect = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                    if (stealableToggle && stealableToggle.checked) {
                        return stealDurationSelect && stealDurationSelect.value !== '';
                    }
                    return true;
                }

                // Update the unified summary card
                function updateSummaryCard() {
                    // Title
                    const titleVal = document.getElementById('titleInput').value.trim() || '—';
                    document.getElementById('summaryTitle').textContent = titleVal;

                    // Price
                    const priceVal = document.getElementById('priceInput').value;
                    document.getElementById('summaryPrice').textContent = priceVal ? '₱' + parseFloat(priceVal).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 }) : '—';

                    // Category
                    const categoryVal = document.getElementById('categoryHidden').value || '—';
                    document.getElementById('summaryCategory').textContent = categoryVal;

                    // Condition
                    const conditionVal = document.getElementById('conditionHidden').value || '—';
                    document.getElementById('summaryCondition').textContent = conditionVal;

                    // Size
                    const sizeVal = document.getElementById('sizeSelect').value || 'Not specified';
                    document.getElementById('summarySize').textContent = sizeVal;

                    // Delivery
                    const opts = [];
                    if (document.getElementById('optDelivery').checked) opts.push('Delivery');
                    if (document.getElementById('optMeetup').checked) opts.push('Halfway');
                    if (document.getElementById('optPickup').checked) opts.push('Pickup');
                    document.getElementById('summaryDelivery').textContent = opts.length ? opts.join(' · ') : 'None selected';

                    // Stealable
                    const toggle = document.getElementById('stealableToggle');
                    const duration = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                    if (toggle && toggle.checked && duration && duration.value) {
                        document.getElementById('summaryStealable').textContent = '⚡ Stealable · ' + duration.value + ' hours';
                    } else {
                        document.getElementById('summaryStealable').textContent = 'Standard listing';
                    }

                    // Description
                    const descVal = document.getElementById('descInput').value.trim();
                    if (descVal) {
                        const truncated = descVal.length > 100 ? descVal.substring(0, 100) + '…' : descVal;
                        document.getElementById('summaryDescription').textContent = truncated;
                    } else {
                        document.getElementById('summaryDescription').textContent = '—';
                    }
                }

                // Show the unified summary and hide all individual fields
                function showUnifiedSummary() {
                    // Hide all field elements
                    fields.forEach(f => {
                        if (f.element) f.element.style.display = 'none';
                    });
                
                    // Hide progress bar
                    document.querySelector('.progressive-progress').style.display = 'none';
                
                    // Show summary card
                    if (listingSummary) {
                        listingSummary.style.display = 'block';
                        updateSummaryCard();
                    }
                
                    if (footerHint) footerHint.textContent = 'Click any row to edit';
                    allFieldsCompleted = true;
                }

                // Hide summary and show fields (when editing)
                function hideSummaryAndShowFields() {
                    fields.forEach(f => {
                        if (f.element) f.element.style.display = '';
                    });
                
                    document.querySelector('.progressive-progress').style.display = '';
                
                    if (listingSummary) listingSummary.style.display = 'none';
                    allFieldsCompleted = false;
                }

                // Edit a specific field from the summary
                function editField(fieldId) {
                    hideSummaryAndShowFields();
                
                    // Collapse all completed fields, expand the target field
                    fields.forEach(f => {
                        if (!f.element) return;
                        const body = f.element.querySelector('.progressive-field__body');
                        const status = f.element.querySelector('.progressive-field__status');
                    
                        f.element.classList.remove('progressive-field--active', 'progressive-field--completed', 'progressive-field--locked');
                    
                        if (completedFields.has(f.id)) {
                            f.element.classList.add('progressive-field--completed');
                            if (body) body.style.display = 'none';
                            if (status) status.textContent = '✓';
                        } else if (f.id === fieldId) {
                            f.element.classList.add('progressive-field--active');
                            if (body) body.style.display = 'block';
                            if (status) status.textContent = '';
                            completedFields.delete(f.id);
                        } else {
                            f.element.classList.add('progressive-field--locked');
                            if (status) status.textContent = '🔒';
                        }
                    });
                
                    // Scroll to the field
                    const targetField = fields.find(f => f.id === fieldId);
                    if (targetField && targetField.element) {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            targetField.element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                            const firstInput = targetField.element.querySelector('input, textarea, select');
                            if (firstInput) firstInput.focus();
                        }, 100);
                    }
                
                    updateProgress();
                }

                // Summary row click handlers
                document.querySelectorAll('[data-edit-field]').forEach(el => {
                    el.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        const fieldId = this.dataset.editField;
                        if (fieldId) {
                            editField(fieldId);
                        }
                    });
                });

                function updateProgress() {
                    const total = fields.length;
                    const completed = completedFields.size;
                    const percent = (completed / total) * 100;
            
                    if (progressFill) {
                        progressFill.style.width = percent + '%';
                    }
                    if (progressText) {
                        progressText.textContent = completed + '/' + total + ' fields complete';
                    }

                    if (completed === total && !allFieldsCompleted) {
                        if (footerHint) footerHint.textContent = 'All fields complete!';
                    } else if (!allFieldsCompleted && footerHint) {
                        const remaining = total - completed;
                        footerHint.textContent = remaining + ' field' + (remaining > 1 ? 's' : '') + ' remaining';
                    }
                }

                function unlockField(fieldId) {
                    const field = fields.find(f => f.id === fieldId);
                    if (!field || !field.element) return;

                    const element = field.element;
                    const body = element.querySelector('.progressive-field__body');
                    const status = element.querySelector('.progressive-field__status');
            
                    element.classList.remove('progressive-field--locked', 'progressive-field--completed');
                    element.classList.add('progressive-field--active');
                    if (body) body.style.display = 'block';
                    if (status) {
                        status.textContent = '';
                        status.style.opacity = '1';
                    }

                    setTimeout(() => {
                        const firstInput = element.querySelector('input, textarea, select, .chip, .pill');
                        if (firstInput) {
                            if (firstInput.classList.contains('chip') || firstInput.classList.contains('pill')) {
                                element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                            } else {
                                firstInput.focus();
                            }
                        }
                        element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                    }, 100);
                }

                function completeField(fieldId) {
                    const field = fields.find(f => f.id === fieldId);
                    if (!field || !field.element) return;

                    const element = field.element;
                    const body = element.querySelector('.progressive-field__body');
                    const status = element.querySelector('.progressive-field__status');
            
                    element.classList.remove('progressive-field--active');
                    element.classList.add('progressive-field--completed');
                
                    if (body) body.style.display = 'none';
                    if (status) status.textContent = '✓';
            
                    completedFields.add(fieldId);
                    updateProgress();
                }

                function tryContinue(currentFieldId, nextFieldId) {
                    const field = fields.find(f => f.id === currentFieldId);
                    if (!field) return false;

                    if (field.validate()) {
                        completeField(currentFieldId);
                
                        if (nextFieldId) {
                            if (nextFieldId === 'summary') {
                                // All fields done - show unified summary
                                completeField(currentFieldId);
                                showUnifiedSummary();
                            } else {
                                unlockField(nextFieldId);
                            }
                        }
                
                        return true;
                    } else {
                        showToast('Please complete this field before continuing.', 'error');
                        return false;
                    }
                }

                // Click on completed field headers to expand for editing
                document.querySelectorAll('.progressive-field .progressive-field__header').forEach(header => {
                    header.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        if (e.target.closest('button') || e.target.closest('input') || e.target.closest('label')) return;
                    
                        const field = this.closest('.progressive-field');
                        if (!field) return;
                    
                        const fieldId = field.dataset.field;
                    
                        if (field.classList.contains('progressive-field--completed')) {
                            const body = field.querySelector('.progressive-field__body');
                            const status = field.querySelector('.progressive-field__status');
                        
                            field.classList.remove('progressive-field--completed');
                            field.classList.add('progressive-field--active');
                            if (body) body.style.display = 'block';
                            if (status) status.textContent = '';
                        
                            completedFields.delete(fieldId);
                            updateProgress();
                        
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                const firstInput = field.querySelector('input, textarea, select');
                                if (firstInput) firstInput.focus();
                            }, 50);
                        }
                    });
                });

                // Continue button handlers
                document.querySelectorAll('.btn--continue').forEach(btn => {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        const fieldElement = this.closest('.progressive-field');
                        if (!fieldElement) return;
                
                        const currentFieldId = fieldElement.dataset.field;
                        const nextFieldId = this.dataset.next;
                
                        tryContinue(currentFieldId, nextFieldId);
                    });
                });

                // Skip button handlers
                document.querySelectorAll('.btn--skip').forEach(btn => {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        const fieldElement = this.closest('.progressive-field');
                        if (!fieldElement) return;
                
                        const currentFieldId = fieldElement.dataset.field;
                        const nextFieldId = this.dataset.next;
                
                        completeField(currentFieldId);
                        if (nextFieldId) {
                            if (nextFieldId === 'summary') {
                                showUnifiedSummary();
                            } else {
                                unlockField(nextFieldId);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                });

                // Enter key support
                document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                        const activeField = document.querySelector('.progressive-field--active');
                        if (activeField) {
                            const continueBtn = activeField.querySelector('.btn--continue');
                            if (continueBtn) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                continueBtn.click();
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });

                // Auto-continue on category/condition selection
                document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    const chip = e.target.closest('.chip');
                    if (chip) {
                        const field = document.getElementById('fieldCategory');
                        if (field && field.classList.contains('progressive-field--active')) {
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                const continueBtn = field.querySelector('.btn--continue');
                                if (continueBtn && validateCategory()) {
                                    continueBtn.click();
                                }
                            }, 150);
                        }
                    }

                    const pill = e.target.closest('.pill');
                    if (pill) {
                        const field = document.getElementById('fieldCondition');
                        if (field && field.classList.contains('progressive-field--active')) {
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                const continueBtn = field.querySelector('.btn--continue');
                                if (continueBtn && validateCondition()) {
                                    continueBtn.click();
                                }
                            }, 150);
                        }
                    }
                });

                // Click on locked field headers to show hint
                document.querySelectorAll('.progressive-field--locked .progressive-field__header').forEach(header => {
                    header.addEventListener('click', function () {
                        showToast('Complete the previous fields first!', 'info');
                    });
                });

                // =========================================================
                // PHOTO UPLOAD
                // =========================================================

                const photoMain = document.getElementById('photoMain');
                let photoInput = document.getElementById('photoInput');
                const photoEmpty = document.getElementById('photoEmpty');
                const photoPreview = document.getElementById('photoPreview');
                const photoMainImg = document.getElementById('photoMainImg');
                const photoStrip = document.getElementById('photoStrip');
                const photoCounter = document.getElementById('photoCounter');

                let selectedFiles = [];
                let objectUrls = [];

                function revokeAll() {
                    objectUrls.forEach(url => URL.revokeObjectURL(url));
                    objectUrls = [];
                }

                function createUrl(file) {
                    const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
                    objectUrls.push(url);
                    return url;
                }

                function renderPreviews() {
                    revokeAll();

                    if (selectedFiles.length > 0) {
                        photoMainImg.src = createUrl(selectedFiles[0]);
                        if (photoPreview) photoPreview.style.display = 'block';
                        if (photoEmpty) photoEmpty.style.display = 'none';
                        if (photoMain) photoMain.classList.add('has-photo');
                    } else {
                        if (photoPreview) photoPreview.style.display = 'none';
                        if (photoEmpty) photoEmpty.style.display = 'flex';
                        if (photoMain) photoMain.classList.remove('has-photo');
                        if (photoMainImg) photoMainImg.src = '';
                    }

                    if (photoStrip) photoStrip.innerHTML = '';

                    selectedFiles.forEach(function (file, i) {
                        const thumb = document.createElement('div');
                        thumb.className = 'strip-thumb' + (i === 0 ? ' strip-thumb--cover' : '');

                        const img = document.createElement('img');
                        img.src = createUrl(file);
                        img.alt = 'Photo ' + (i + 1);

                        const removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
                        removeBtn.type = 'button';
                        removeBtn.className = 'strip-thumb__remove';
                        removeBtn.dataset.index = String(i);
                        removeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Remove photo ' + (i + 1));
                        removeBtn.textContent = '×';

                        thumb.appendChild(img);
                        thumb.appendChild(removeBtn);
                        if (photoStrip) photoStrip.appendChild(thumb);
                    });

                    if (selectedFiles.length < 5 && photoStrip) {
                        const addSlot = document.createElement('div');
                        addSlot.className = 'strip-add';
                        addSlot.setAttribute('role', 'button');
                        addSlot.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
                        addSlot.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Add another photo');
                        addSlot.textContent = '+';
                        addSlot.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            if (photoInput) photoInput.click();
                        });
                        addSlot.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                            if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                if (photoInput) photoInput.click();
                            }
                        });
                        photoStrip.appendChild(addSlot);
                    }

                    const oldInput = photoInput;
                    const newInput = document.createElement('input');
                    newInput.type = 'file';
                    newInput.id = 'photoInput';
                    newInput.name = 'Images';
                    newInput.multiple = true;
                    newInput.accept = 'image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp';
                    newInput.className = 'photo-file-input';
            
                    const dt = new DataTransfer();
                    selectedFiles.forEach(f => dt.items.add(f));
                    newInput.files = dt.files;
            
                    newInput.addEventListener('change', function (e) {
                        if (e.target.files.length > 0) {
                            addFiles(e.target.files);
                        }
                        e.target.value = '';
                    });
            
                    if (oldInput && oldInput.parentNode) {
                        oldInput.parentNode.replaceChild(newInput, oldInput);
                    }
                    photoInput = newInput;

                    if (photoCounter) {
                        photoCounter.textContent = selectedFiles.length + ' / 5';
                    }
                }

                function addFiles(files) {
                    const remaining = 5 - selectedFiles.length;
                    const toAdd = Array.from(files).slice(0, remaining);

                    toAdd.forEach(function (file) {
                        if (!file.type.match(/^image\/(jpeg|png|webp)$/)) {
                            showToast((file.name || 'File') + ' is not a supported format.', 'error');
                            return;
                        }
                        if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                            showToast((file.name || 'File') + ' exceeds 5 MB.', 'error');
                            return;
                        }
                        selectedFiles.push(file);
                    });

                    renderPreviews();
                }

                function removeFile(index) {
                    selectedFiles.splice(index, 1);
                    renderPreviews();
                }

                if (photoMain) {
                    photoMain.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        photoMain.classList.add('is-dragging');
                    });

                    photoMain.addEventListener('dragleave', function (e) {
                        if (!photoMain.contains(e.relatedTarget)) {
                            photoMain.classList.remove('is-dragging');
                        }
                    });

                    photoMain.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        photoMain.classList.remove('is-dragging');
                        if (e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {
                            addFiles(e.dataTransfer.files);
                        }
                    });

                    photoMain.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            if (photoInput) photoInput.click();
                        }
                    });
                }

                if (photoInput) {
                    photoInput.addEventListener('change', function (e) {
                        if (e.target.files.length > 0) {
                            addFiles(e.target.files);
                        }
                        photoInput.value = '';
                    });
                }

                if (photoStrip) {
                    photoStrip.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                        const btn = e.target.closest('.strip-thumb__remove');
                        if (btn) {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            removeFile(parseInt(btn.dataset.index, 10));
                            return;
                        }
        
                        const thumb = e.target.closest('.strip-thumb');
                        if (thumb) {
                            const index = Array.from(photoStrip.children).indexOf(thumb);
                            if (index >= 0 && index < selectedFiles.length) {
                                const file = selectedFiles.splice(index, 1)[0];
                                selectedFiles.unshift(file);
                                renderPreviews();
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }

                renderPreviews();

                // =========================================================
                // CHARACTER COUNTERS
                // =========================================================

                function bindCounter(inputId, counterId, max) {
                    const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
                    const counter = document.getElementById(counterId);
                    if (!input || !counter) return;
                    function update() {
                        const len = input.value.length;
                        counter.textContent = len + '/' + max;
                        counter.classList.toggle('field__counter--warn', len > max * 0.9);
                    }
                    input.addEventListener('input', update);
                    update();
                }

                bindCounter('titleInput', 'titleCounter', 100);
                bindCounter('descInput', 'descCounter', 1000);

                // =========================================================
                // CATEGORY CHIPS
                // =========================================================

                const categoryChips = document.getElementById('categoryChips');
                const categoryHidden = document.getElementById('categoryHidden');

                if (categoryChips && categoryHidden) {
                    categoryChips.querySelectorAll('.chip').forEach(function (chip) {
                        chip.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            categoryChips.querySelectorAll('.chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('chip--active'));
                            chip.classList.add('chip--active');
                            categoryHidden.value = chip.dataset.value;
                        });
                    });
                }

                // =========================================================
                // CONDITION PILLS
                // =========================================================

                const conditionPills = document.getElementById('conditionPills');
                const conditionHidden = document.getElementById('conditionHidden');

                if (conditionPills && conditionHidden) {
                    conditionPills.querySelectorAll('.pill').forEach(function (pill) {
                        pill.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            conditionPills.querySelectorAll('.pill').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('pill--active'));
                            pill.classList.add('pill--active');
                            conditionHidden.value = pill.dataset.value;
                        });
                    });
                }

                // =========================================================
                // DELIVERY OPTIONS
                // =========================================================

                document.querySelectorAll('.delivery-input').forEach(function (checkbox) {
                    checkbox.addEventListener('change', function () {
                        const err = document.getElementById('fulfillmentError');
                        if (err) err.textContent = '';
                        const grid = document.getElementById('deliveryGrid');
                        if (grid) grid.classList.remove('delivery-error-flash');
                    });
                });

                // =========================================================
                // STEALABLE TOGGLE
                // =========================================================

                const stealableToggle = document.getElementById('stealableToggle');
                const stealDurationPanel = document.getElementById('stealDurationPanel');
                const stealDurationSelect = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');

                if (stealableToggle && stealDurationPanel) {
                    function syncStealPanel() {
                        if (stealableToggle.checked) {
                            stealDurationPanel.classList.add('is-visible');
                        } else {
                            stealDurationPanel.classList.remove('is-visible');
                            if (stealDurationSelect) stealDurationSelect.value = '';
                        }
                    }
                    stealableToggle.addEventListener('change', syncStealPanel);
                    syncStealPanel();
                }

                // =========================================================
                // FORM SUBMIT
                // =========================================================

                const form = document.getElementById('createItemForm');
                const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');

                if (form) {
                    form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                        let hasError = false;
                
                        if (!validateTitle()) {
                            showToast('Please enter a title.', 'error');
                            hasError = true;
                        } else if (!validatePrice()) {
                            showToast('Please enter a valid price.', 'error');
                            hasError = true;
                        } else if (!validateCategory()) {
                            showToast('Please select a category.', 'error');
                            hasError = true;
                        } else if (!validateCondition()) {
                            showToast('Please select the condition.', 'error');
                            hasError = true;
                        } else if (!validateDescription()) {
                            showToast('Please enter a description.', 'error');
                            hasError = true;
                        } else if (!validateDelivery()) {
                            showToast('Please select at least one delivery option.', 'error');
                            hasError = true;
                        }

                        if (hasError) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            editField('title');
                            return false;
                        }

                        if (stealableToggle && stealableToggle.checked &&
                            stealDurationSelect && !stealDurationSelect.value) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            showToast('Please select a steal window duration.', 'error');
                            editField('stealable');
                            return false;
                        }

                        if (submitBtn) {
                            submitBtn.disabled = true;
                            const span = submitBtn.querySelector('span');
                            if (span) span.textContent = 'Publishing...';
                        }
                    });
                }

                // =========================================================
                // TOAST HELPER
                // =========================================================

                function showToast(message, type) {
                    type = type || 'info';
                    const toast = document.createElement('div');
                    toast.className = 'app-toast app-toast--' + type;
                    toast.textContent = message;
                    document.body.appendChild(toast);
                    setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 3200);
                }

                // Initialize progress
                updateProgress();
        
                const titleField = document.getElementById('fieldTitle');
                if (titleField) {
                    titleField.classList.add('progressive-field--active');
                }

                // =========================================================
                // SCROLL TO TOP
                // =========================================================
        
                let scrollTopBtn = document.getElementById('scrollTopBtn');
        
                if (!scrollTopBtn) {
                    scrollTopBtn = document.createElement('button');
                    scrollTopBtn.id = 'scrollTopBtn';
                    scrollTopBtn.className = 'scroll-top-btn';
                    scrollTopBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Scroll to top');
                    scrollTopBtn.innerHTML = `
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                            <path d="M5 12l5-5 5 5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                        </svg>
                    `;
                    document.body.appendChild(scrollTopBtn);
                }
        
                function scrollToTop() {
                    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
                }
        
                scrollTopBtn.addEventListener('click', scrollToTop);
        
                window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                    if (window.scrollY > 300) {
                        scrollTopBtn.classList.add('visible');
                    } else {
                        scrollTopBtn.classList.remove('visible');
                    }
                });
            })();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

--- Views\Items\Delete.cshtml ---
﻿@model ThriftLoop.Models.Item
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Delete Listing";
    Layout = null;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Items.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />

<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="container">
        <div class="confirm-shell">
            <div class="confirm-card">
                <div class="confirm-card__icon">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M12 9v3.75m-9.303 3.376c-.866 1.5.217 3.374 1.948 3.374h14.71c1.73 0 2.813-1.874 1.948-3.374L13.949 3.378c-.866-1.5-3.032-1.5-3.898 0L2.697 16.126zM12 15.75h.007v.008H12v-.008z" />
                    </svg>
                </div>

                <h1 class="confirm-card__title">Delete this listing?</h1>
                <p class="confirm-card__body">
                    This action is permanent and cannot be undone.
                </p>

                <div class="confirm-item">
                    @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.ImageUrl))
                    {
                        <img src="@Model.ImageUrl" alt="@Model.Title" class="confirm-item__img" />
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <div class="confirm-item__img confirm-item__img--placeholder">

                                <circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="1.5" />
                                <path d="M21 15l-5-5L5 21" />
                            </svg>
                        </div>
                    }
                    <div>
                        <p class="confirm-item__title">@Model.Title</p>
                        <p class="confirm-item__price">₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2")</p>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="confirm-actions">
                    <a asp-action="Index" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                    <form asp-action="Delete" asp-route-id="@Model.Id" method="post" id="deleteForm">
                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn--danger" id="deleteBtn">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.75 1A2.75 2.75 0 006 3.75v.443c-.795.077-1.584.176-2.365.298a.75.75 0 10.23 1.482l.149-.022.841 10.518A2.75 2.75 0 007.596 19h4.807a2.75 2.75 0 002.742-2.53l.841-10.52.149.023a.75.75 0 00.23-1.482A41.03 41.03 0 0014 4.193V3.75A2.75 2.75 0 0011.25 1h-2.5zM10 4c.84 0 1.673.025 2.5.075V3.75c0-.69-.56-1.25-1.25-1.25h-2.5c-.69 0-1.25.56-1.25 1.25v.325C8.327 4.025 9.16 4 10 4zM8.58 7.72a.75.75 0 00-1.5.06l.3 7.5a.75.75 0 101.5-.06l-.3-7.5zm4.34.06a.75.75 0 10-1.5-.06l-.3 7.5a.75.75 0 101.5.06l.3-7.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                            </svg>
                            Yes, Delete
                        </button>
                    </form>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
            document.getElementById('deleteForm')?.addEventListener('submit', function() {
                const btn = document.getElementById('deleteBtn');
                btn.disabled = true;
                btn.textContent = 'Deleting...';
            });
    </script>
</body>

--- Views\Items\Details.cshtml ---
﻿@model ThriftLoop.Models.Item
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = Model.Title;
    Layout = null;

    bool isOwner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOwner ?? false);
    bool isAnonymous = (bool)(ViewBag.IsAnonymous ?? true);
    bool isCurrentWinner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsCurrentWinner ?? false);
    bool isOriginalGetter = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOriginalGetter ?? false);

    bool isStealable = Model.ListingType == ListingType.Stealable;
    bool stealWindowOpen = isStealable
                           && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved
                           && Model.StealEndsAt.HasValue
                           && DateTime.UtcNow <= Model.StealEndsAt.Value;

    string sellerDisplay = Model.User is not null
        ? Model.User.Email.Split('@')[0]
        : "Unknown seller";

    string condClass = Model.Condition switch
    {
        "New" => "detail-condition--new",
        "Like New" => "detail-condition--like-new",
        "Good" => "detail-condition--good",
        "Fair" => "detail-condition--fair",
        _ => "detail-condition--poor"
    };

    string priceLabel = isStealable ? "Starting price" : "Fixed price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved)
        priceLabel = "Current price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
        priceLabel = "Stolen price";

    bool hasImages = Model.ImageUrls.Count > 0;
    
    // Determine default fulfillment method (first allowed option)
    string defaultFulfillmentMethod = Model.AllowDelivery ? "Delivery"
        : Model.AllowHalfway ? "Halfway"
        : Model.AllowPickup ? "Pickup"
        : "Delivery";
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Items.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="detail-shell">

        <nav class="detail-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">
            <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="detail-breadcrumb__link">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                </svg>
                Back to listings
            </a>
        </nav>

        <div class="detail-grid">

            <aside class="detail-img-col">
                <div class="detail-gallery">
                    <div class="detail-img-frame" id="galleryMain">
                        @if (hasImages)
                        {
                            <img src="@Model.ImageUrls[0]"
                                 id="mainGalleryImg"
                                 alt="Photo of @Model.Title"
                                 class="detail-img"
                                 loading="eager" />

                            @if (Model.ImageUrls.Count > 1)
                            {
                                <button type="button" class="gallery-arrow gallery-arrow--prev" id="galleryPrev" aria-label="Previous photo">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="18" height="18">
                                        <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                                <button type="button" class="gallery-arrow gallery-arrow--next" id="galleryNext" aria-label="Next photo">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="18" height="18">
                                        <path d="M7.5 5L12.5 10L7.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                                <span class="gallery-counter" id="galleryCounter">
                                    1 / @Model.ImageUrls.Count
                                </span>
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="detail-img detail-img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                    <rect x="6" y="10" width="52" height="44" rx="6" />
                                    <circle cx="22" cy="26" r="6" />
                                    <path d="M6 46l16-14 10 10 8-7 18 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                </svg>
                                <span>No photo</span>
                            </div>
                        }

                        @if (isStealable)
                        {
                            <span class="detail-stealable-badge" aria-label="Stealable listing">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M8.75 3.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v2.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 000 1.5h2.5v2.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-2.5h2.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-2.5v-2.5z" />
                                </svg>
                                Stealable
                            </span>
                        }
                    </div>

                    @if (Model.ImageUrls.Count > 1)
                    {
                        <div class="gallery-thumbs" id="galleryThumbs" role="list">
                            @for (int t = 0; t < Model.ImageUrls.Count; t++)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="gallery-thumb @(t == 0 ? "gallery-thumb--active" : "")"
                                        data-index="@t"
                                        data-src="@Model.ImageUrls[t]"
                                        role="listitem"
                                        aria-label="Photo @(t + 1)">
                                    <img src="@Model.ImageUrls[t]" alt="Thumbnail @(t + 1)" loading="lazy" />
                                    @if (t == 0)
                                    {
                                        <span class="gallery-thumb__cover">Cover</span>
                                    }
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                    }
                </div>

                <div class="detail-seller detail-seller--below-img">
                    <div class="detail-seller__avatar" aria-hidden="true">
                        @sellerDisplay.Substring(0, 1).ToUpper()
                    </div>
                    <div class="detail-seller__info">
                        <p class="detail-seller__label">Listed by</p>
                        <p class="detail-seller__name">@sellerDisplay</p>
                        <p class="detail-seller__since">
                            Member since @(Model.User?.CreatedAt.ToString("MMMM yyyy") ?? "—")
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </aside>

            <section class="detail-info-col">
                <div class="detail-meta-row">
                    <span class="detail-category">@Model.Category</span>
                    <span class="detail-condition @condClass">@Model.Condition</span>
                    @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.Size))
                    {
                        <span class="detail-size">@Model.Size</span>
                    }
                    @if (isStealable)
                    {
                        <span class="detail-listing-type-badge">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                <path d="M7 1a6 6 0 100 12A6 6 0 007 1zm.6 8.9H6.4V6.4h1.2v3.5zm0-4.6H6.4V4.1h1.2v1.2z" />
                            </svg>
                            Stealable
                        </span>
                    }
                </div>

                <h1 class="detail-title">@Model.Title</h1>

                <div class="detail-price-block">
                    <span class="detail-price">₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2")</span>
                    <span class="detail-price-label">@priceLabel</span>
                    @if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Available)
                    {
                        <span class="detail-steal-note">+₱50 if stolen</span>
                    }
                </div>

                @* Fulfillment Options Display (show what seller allows) *@
                <div class="detail-fulfillment-badges">
                    @if (Model.AllowDelivery)
                    {
                        <span class="fulfillment-badge fulfillment-badge--delivery">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12">

    <script>
            window.itemDetailsData = {
                itemId: @Model.Id,
                imageUrls: @Json.Serialize(Model.ImageUrls),
                stealEndsAt: '@(Model.StealEndsAt.HasValue ? DateTime.SpecifyKind(Model.StealEndsAt.Value, DateTimeKind.Utc).ToString("O") : "")',
                finalizeDeadline: '@(Model.FinalizeDeadline.HasValue ? DateTime.SpecifyKind(Model.FinalizeDeadline.Value, DateTimeKind.Utc).ToString("O") : "")'
            };

            // Fulfillment method selection - switches between Buy Now and Contact Seller
            (function() {
                'use strict';
            
                const fulfillmentRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-fulfillment-radio');
                const fulfillmentInput = document.getElementById('fulfillmentMethodInput');
                const deliveryFeeRow = document.getElementById('deliveryFeeRow');
                const totalPriceDisplay = document.getElementById('totalPriceDisplay');
                const fulfillmentOptions = document.querySelectorAll('.detail-fulfillment-option');
                const buyNowForm = document.getElementById('buyNowForm');
                const contactSellerForm = document.getElementById('contactSellerForm');
                const fulfillmentHint = document.getElementById('fulfillmentHint');
            
                const itemPrice = @Model.Price;
                const deliveryFee = 50.00;
            
                function updateFulfillmentUI(method) {
                    // Update option selection styling
                    fulfillmentOptions.forEach(function(opt) {
                        opt.classList.remove('detail-fulfillment-option--selected');
                    });
                
                    const selectedOption = document.querySelector('.detail-fulfillment-option[data-method="' + method + '"]');
                    if (selectedOption) {
                        selectedOption.classList.add('detail-fulfillment-option--selected');
                    }
                
                    const isDelivery = method === 'Delivery';
                    const isHalfway = method === 'Halfway';
                    const isPickup = method === 'Pickup';
                
                    // Show/hide delivery fee row
                    if (deliveryFeeRow) {
                        deliveryFeeRow.style.display = isDelivery ? 'flex' : 'none';
                    }
                
                    // Calculate and update total price
                    const total = isDelivery ? itemPrice + deliveryFee : itemPrice;
                    if (totalPriceDisplay) {
                        totalPriceDisplay.textContent = '₱' + total.toFixed(2).replace(/\d(?=(\d{3})+\.)/g, '$&,');
                    }
                
                    // Update hidden input
                    if (fulfillmentInput) {
                        fulfillmentInput.value = method;
                    }
                
                    // Toggle between Buy Now and Contact Seller forms
                    if (buyNowForm && contactSellerForm) {
                        if (isDelivery) {
                            buyNowForm.style.display = 'block';
                            contactSellerForm.style.display = 'none';
                            if (fulfillmentHint) {
                                fulfillmentHint.textContent = 'Proceed to checkout — rider will deliver this item.';
                            }
                        } else {
                            buyNowForm.style.display = 'none';
                            contactSellerForm.style.display = 'block';
                            if (fulfillmentHint) {
                                fulfillmentHint.textContent = isHalfway
                                    ? 'Chat with the seller to coordinate a halfway meetup.'
                                    : 'Chat with the seller to arrange pickup details.';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            
                if (fulfillmentRadios.length > 0) {
                    fulfillmentRadios.forEach(function(radio) {
                        radio.addEventListener('change', function() {
                            updateFulfillmentUI(radio.value);
                        });
                    });
                
                    fulfillmentOptions.forEach(function(opt) {
                        opt.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                            const radio = this.querySelector('.detail-fulfillment-radio');
                            if (radio && !radio.disabled) {
                                radio.checked = true;
                                updateFulfillmentUI(radio.value);
                            }
                        });
                    });
                
                    // Initialize UI with default selection
                    const checkedFulfillment = document.querySelector('.detail-fulfillment-radio:checked');
                    if (checkedFulfillment) {
                        updateFulfillmentUI(checkedFulfillment.value);
                    } else {
                        // Default to first available option
                        const firstOption = document.querySelector('.detail-fulfillment-radio');
                        if (firstOption) {
                            firstOption.checked = true;
                            updateFulfillmentUI(firstOption.value);
                        }
                    }
                }
            })();
    </script>
    <script src="~/js/items-details.js" asp-append-version="true"></script>
</body>
</html>
