                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="12" height="12">
                                            <path d="M4 6L8 10L12 6" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                        </svg>
                                    </span>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 4: Delivery -->
                            <div class="summary-section">
                                <div class="inline-field" data-field="delivery">
                                    <span class="inline-field__label">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                            <rect x="1.5" y="7.5" width="13" height="5.5" rx="1" />
                                            <circle cx="5" cy="13" r="1" />
                                            <circle cx="11" cy="13" r="1" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Delivery
                                    </span>
                                    <div class="inline-field__content">
                                        <span class="inline-field__display" id="deliveryDisplay">
                                            @{
                                                var deliveryOpts = new List<string>();
                                                if (Model.AllowDelivery) deliveryOpts.Add("Delivery");
                                                if (Model.AllowHalfway) deliveryOpts.Add("Halfway");
                                                if (Model.AllowPickup) deliveryOpts.Add("Pickup");
                                            }
                                            @(deliveryOpts.Any() ? string.Join(" · ", deliveryOpts) : "None selected")
                                        </span>
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="inline-field__chevron">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="12" height="12">
                                            <path d="M4 6L8 10L12 6" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                        </svg>
                                    </span>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Row 5: Description -->
                            <div class="summary-section">
                                <div class="inline-field inline-field--textarea" data-field="description">
                                    <span class="inline-field__label">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14">
                                            <rect x="1.5" y="2.5" width="13" height="11" rx="1" />
                                            <path d="M4.5 6H11.5" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                            <path d="M4.5 8.5H9.5" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Description
                                    </span>
                                    <div class="inline-field__content">
                                        <span class="inline-field__display inline-field__display--desc" id="descriptionDisplay">
                                            @{
                                                var desc = Model.Description ?? "";
                                                var truncated = desc.Length > 80 ? desc.Substring(0, 80) + "…" : desc;
                                            }
                                            @(string.IsNullOrEmpty(desc) ? "—" : truncated)
                                        </span>
                                        <textarea asp-for="Description" class="inline-field__textarea" id="descInput" rows="1" placeholder="Describe your item..." maxlength="1000" style="display: none;">@Model.Description</textarea>
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="inline-field__counter" id="descCounter">@(Model.Description?.Length ?? 0)/1000</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <!-- Save Actions -->
                            <div class="summary-card__footer">
                                <span class="form-error" id="deliveryError"></span>
                                <a asp-action="Index" class="btn btn--secondary">Cancel</a>
                                <button type="submit" class="btn btn--primary" id="submitBtn">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path d="M3 10h14M10 3l7 7-7 7" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                    <span>Save Changes</span>
                                </button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>

    <!-- Floating Selection Panel -->
    <div class="floating-panel" id="floatingPanel" style="display: none;">
        <div class="floating-panel__content" id="floatingPanelContent"></div>
    </div>

    <!-- Floating Delivery Panel -->
    <div class="floating-panel floating-panel--large" id="deliveryPanel" style="display: none;">
        <div class="floating-panel__header">
            <span>Delivery Options</span>
            <button type="button" class="floating-panel__close" id="closeDeliveryPanel">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="16" height="16">
                    <path d="M5 5L15 15M15 5L5 15" stroke-linecap="round" />
                </svg>
            </button>
        </div>
        <div class="floating-panel__body">
            <label class="delivery-checkbox @(Model.AllowDelivery ? "delivery-checkbox--checked" : "")">
                <input type="checkbox" asp-for="AllowDelivery" />
                <span class="delivery-checkbox__icon">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="18" height="18">
                        <rect x="2.5" y="9.5" width="15" height="7" rx="1" />
                        <circle cx="6" cy="16.5" r="1.5" />
                        <circle cx="14" cy="16.5" r="1.5" />
                    </svg>
                </span>
                <div>
                    <span class="delivery-checkbox__title">Delivery</span>
                    <span class="delivery-checkbox__desc">Ship directly to buyer</span>
                </div>
            </label>
            <label class="delivery-checkbox @(Model.AllowHalfway ? "delivery-checkbox--checked" : "")">
                <input type="checkbox" asp-for="AllowHalfway" />
                <span class="delivery-checkbox__icon">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="18" height="18">
                        <circle cx="10" cy="10" r="7.5" />
                        <path d="M10 5v5l3 3" stroke-linecap="round" />
                    </svg>
                </span>
                <div>
                    <span class="delivery-checkbox__title">Halfway Meetup</span>
                    <span class="delivery-checkbox__desc">Meet at agreed location</span>
                </div>
            </label>
            <label class="delivery-checkbox @(Model.AllowPickup ? "delivery-checkbox--checked" : "")">
                <input type="checkbox" asp-for="AllowPickup" />
                <span class="delivery-checkbox__icon">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="18" height="18">
                        <path d="M3 9.5L10 3.5L17 9.5V16.5H3V9.5Z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                        <rect x="8" y="11" width="4" height="5.5" />
                    </svg>
                </span>
                <div>
                    <span class="delivery-checkbox__title">Pickup</span>
                    <span class="delivery-checkbox__desc">Buyer comes to you</span>
                </div>
            </label>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="floating-overlay" id="floatingOverlay" style="display: none;"></div>

    <script>
        window.itemEditData = {
            existingImageUrls: @Json.Serialize(Model.ExistingImageUrls)
        };
    
        // Pre-defined options
        window.editOptions = {
            categories: @Json.Serialize(ItemEditViewModel.Categories),
            conditions: @Json.Serialize(ItemEditViewModel.Conditions),
            sizes: @Json.Serialize(ItemEditViewModel.Sizes)
        };
    </script>
    <script>
        (function() {
            'use strict';

            // =========================================================
            // STATE MANAGEMENT
            // =========================================================
        
            const floatingPanel = document.getElementById('floatingPanel');
            const floatingPanelContent = document.getElementById('floatingPanelContent');
            const deliveryPanel = document.getElementById('deliveryPanel');
            const floatingOverlay = document.getElementById('floatingOverlay');
            const closeDeliveryPanel = document.getElementById('closeDeliveryPanel');
        
            let currentField = null;
            let originalValues = {};
        
            // Show floating panel
            function showFloatingPanel(anchor, content, position = 'bottom') {
                const rect = anchor.getBoundingClientRect();
                floatingPanelContent.innerHTML = content;
                floatingPanel.style.display = 'block';
            
                const panelRect = floatingPanel.getBoundingClientRect();
                let top = rect.bottom + 8;
                let left = rect.left;
            
                if (position === 'top' || top + panelRect.height > window.innerHeight - 20) {
                    top = rect.top - panelRect.height - 8;
                }
            
                if (left + panelRect.width > window.innerWidth - 20) {
                    left = window.innerWidth - panelRect.width - 20;
                }
            
                floatingPanel.style.top = top + 'px';
                floatingPanel.style.left = Math.max(20, left) + 'px';
                floatingOverlay.style.display = 'block';
            }
        
            function showDeliveryPanel(anchor) {
                const rect = anchor.getBoundingClientRect();
                deliveryPanel.style.display = 'block';
            
                const panelRect = deliveryPanel.getBoundingClientRect();
                let top = rect.bottom + 8;
                let left = rect.left;
            
                if (top + panelRect.height > window.innerHeight - 20) {
                    top = rect.top - panelRect.height - 8;
                }
            
                if (left + panelRect.width > window.innerWidth - 20) {
                    left = window.innerWidth - panelRect.width - 20;
                }
            
                deliveryPanel.style.top = top + 'px';
                deliveryPanel.style.left = Math.max(20, left) + 'px';
                floatingOverlay.style.display = 'block';
                currentField = 'delivery';
            }
        
            function hideAllPanels() {
                floatingPanel.style.display = 'none';
                deliveryPanel.style.display = 'none';
                floatingOverlay.style.display = 'none';
            
                if (currentField) {
                    const field = document.querySelector(`[data-field="${currentField}"]`);
                    if (field) field.classList.remove('is-active');
                }
                currentField = null;
            }
        
            // Build bubble panel content (horizontal bubbles)
            function buildBubblePanel(options, selectedValue, fieldType, allowClear = false) {
                let clearButton = '';
                if (allowClear) {
                    clearButton = `<button type="button" class="bubble-panel__clear" data-clear="true">Clear</button>`;
                }
                return `
                    <div class="bubble-panel">
                        ${options.map(opt => `
                            <button type="button" class="bubble-panel__item ${selectedValue === opt ? 'bubble-panel__item--selected' : ''}" data-value="${opt}">
                                ${opt}
                            </button>
                        `).join('')}
                        ${clearButton}
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        
            // Handle field clicks
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-field]').forEach(field => {
                field.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    if (e.target.closest('input') || e.target.closest('textarea')) return;
                
                    const fieldId = this.dataset.field;
                    const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();
                
                    // Remove active from others
                    document.querySelectorAll('[data-field]').forEach(f => f.classList.remove('is-active'));
                    this.classList.add('is-active');
                
                    // Handle different field types
                    if (fieldId === 'category') {
                        const selected = document.getElementById('categoryHidden').value;
                        showFloatingPanel(this, buildBubblePanel(window.editOptions.categories, selected, 'category'));
                        currentField = 'category';
                    
                        // Attach bubble listeners
                        document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(bubble => {
                            bubble.addEventListener('click', function() {
                                const value = this.dataset.value;
                                document.getElementById('categoryHidden').value = value;
                                document.getElementById('categoryDisplay').textContent = value;
                                document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bubble-panel__item--selected'));
                                this.classList.add('bubble-panel__item--selected');
                                setTimeout(hideAllPanels, 100);
                            });
                        });
                    
                    } else if (fieldId === 'condition') {
                        const selected = document.getElementById('conditionHidden').value;
                        showFloatingPanel(this, buildBubblePanel(window.editOptions.conditions, selected, 'condition'));
                        currentField = 'condition';
                    
                        document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(bubble => {
                            bubble.addEventListener('click', function() {
                                const value = this.dataset.value;
                                document.getElementById('conditionHidden').value = value;
                                document.getElementById('conditionDisplay').textContent = value;
                                document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bubble-panel__item--selected'));
                                this.classList.add('bubble-panel__item--selected');
                                setTimeout(hideAllPanels, 100);
                            });
                        });
                    
                    } else if (fieldId === 'size') {
                        const selected = document.getElementById('sizeSelect').value;
                        showFloatingPanel(this, buildBubblePanel(window.editOptions.sizes, selected, 'size', true));
                        currentField = 'size';
                    
                        document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(bubble => {
                            bubble.addEventListener('click', function() {
                                const value = this.dataset.value;
                                document.getElementById('sizeSelect').value = value;
                                document.getElementById('sizeDisplay').textContent = value || 'Not specified';
                                document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bubble-panel__item--selected'));
                                this.classList.add('bubble-panel__item--selected');
                                setTimeout(hideAllPanels, 100);
                            });
                        });
                        
                        const clearBtn = document.querySelector('.bubble-panel__clear');
                        if (clearBtn) {
                            clearBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                                document.getElementById('sizeSelect').value = '';
                                document.getElementById('sizeDisplay').textContent = 'Not specified';
                                document.querySelectorAll('.bubble-panel__item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bubble-panel__item--selected'));
                                setTimeout(hideAllPanels, 100);
                            });
                        }
                    
                    } else if (fieldId === 'delivery') {
                        showDeliveryPanel(this);
                    
                    } else if (fieldId === 'title') {
                        const display = document.getElementById('titleDisplay');
                        const input = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                        const counter = document.getElementById('titleCounter');
                    
                        originalValues.title = display.textContent === '—' ? '' : display.textContent;
                    
                        display.style.display = 'none';
                        input.style.display = 'block';
                        input.focus();
                        currentField = 'title';
                    
                        const saveTitle = () => {
                            const val = input.value.trim();
                            display.textContent = val || '—';
                            counter.textContent = (val?.length || 0) + '/100';
                            display.style.display = 'block';
                            input.style.display = 'none';
                            this.classList.remove('is-active');
                            currentField = null;
                        };
                    
                        input.onblur = saveTitle;
                        input.onkeydown = (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); saveTitle(); } };
                    
                    } else if (fieldId === 'price') {
                        const display = document.getElementById('priceDisplay');
                        const wrapper = document.querySelector('.inline-field__price-input');
                        const input = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                    
                        originalValues.price = display.textContent === '—' ? '' : display.textContent.replace('₱', '').replace(/,/g, '');
                    
                        display.style.display = 'none';
                        wrapper.style.display = 'flex';
                        input.focus();
                        currentField = 'price';
                    
                        const savePrice = () => {
                            const val = input.value;
                            display.textContent = val ? '₱' + parseFloat(val).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 }) : '—';
                            display.style.display = 'block';
                            wrapper.style.display = 'none';
                            this.classList.remove('is-active');
                            currentField = null;
                        };
                    
                        input.onblur = savePrice;
                        input.onkeydown = (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); savePrice(); } };
                    
                    } else if (fieldId === 'description') {
                        const display = document.getElementById('descriptionDisplay');
                        const textarea = document.getElementById('descInput');
                        const counter = document.getElementById('descCounter');
                    
                        originalValues.description = textarea.value;
                    
                        display.style.display = 'none';
                        textarea.style.display = 'block';
                        textarea.style.height = '80px';
                        textarea.focus();
                        currentField = 'description';
                    
                        const saveDescription = () => {
                            const val = textarea.value.trim();
                            display.textContent = val ? (val.length > 80 ? val.substring(0, 80) + '…' : val) : '—';
                            counter.textContent = (textarea.value?.length || 0) + '/1000';
                            display.style.display = 'block';
                            textarea.style.display = 'none';
                            this.classList.remove('is-active');
                            currentField = null;
                        };
                    
                        textarea.onblur = saveDescription;
                    }
                });
            });
        
            // Delivery checkboxes
            document.querySelectorAll('.delivery-checkbox input').forEach(cb => {
                cb.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    const label = this.closest('.delivery-checkbox');
                    if (this.checked) {
                        label.classList.add('delivery-checkbox--checked');
                    } else {
                        label.classList.remove('delivery-checkbox--checked');
                    }
                    updateDeliveryDisplay();
                });
            });
        
            function updateDeliveryDisplay() {
                const opts = [];
                if (document.querySelector('[name="AllowDelivery"]')?.checked) opts.push('Delivery');
                if (document.querySelector('[name="AllowHalfway"]')?.checked) opts.push('Halfway');
                if (document.querySelector('[name="AllowPickup"]')?.checked) opts.push('Pickup');
                document.getElementById('deliveryDisplay').textContent = opts.length ? opts.join(' · ') : 'None selected';
            }
        
            // Close panels
            floatingOverlay.addEventListener('click', hideAllPanels);
            if (closeDeliveryPanel) {
                closeDeliveryPanel.addEventListener('click', hideAllPanels);
            }
        
            document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Escape') hideAllPanels();
            });
        
            // Character counters
            const titleInput = document.getElementById('titleInput');
            const titleCounter = document.getElementById('titleCounter');
            if (titleInput) {
                titleInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
                    titleCounter.textContent = (titleInput.value?.length || 0) + '/100';
                });
            }
        
            const descInput = document.getElementById('descInput');
            const descCounter = document.getElementById('descCounter');
            if (descInput) {
                descInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
                    descCounter.textContent = (descInput.value?.length || 0) + '/1000';
                });
            }

            // =========================================================
            // PHOTO MANAGEMENT
            // =========================================================
        
            const photoUploadArea = document.getElementById('photoUploadArea');
            const photoInput = document.getElementById('photoInput');
            const existingPhotos = document.getElementById('existingPhotos');
            const newPhotos = document.getElementById('newPhotos');
            const removedContainer = document.getElementById('removedImagesContainer');
            const photoCount = document.getElementById('photoCount');
            const existingUrlsHidden = document.getElementById('existingImageUrlsHidden');
        
            let existingImageUrls = window.itemEditData?.existingImageUrls || [];
            let newImageFiles = [];
        
            function updatePhotoCount() {
                const total = existingImageUrls.length + newImageFiles.length;
                if (photoCount) photoCount.textContent = total + ' / 5';
            }
        
            function updateExistingUrlsHidden() {
                if (existingUrlsHidden) {
                    existingUrlsHidden.value = JSON.stringify(existingImageUrls);
                }
            }
        
            function addRemovedInput(url) {
                const input = document.createElement('input');
                input.type = 'hidden';
                input.name = 'RemovedImageUrls';
                input.value = url;
                removedContainer.appendChild(input);
            }
        
            function removeExistingPhoto(url, element) {
                const index = existingImageUrls.indexOf(url);
                if (index > -1) {
                    existingImageUrls.splice(index, 1);
                    addRemovedInput(url);
                    element.remove();
                    updatePhotoCount();
                    updateExistingUrlsHidden();
                }
            }
        
            function renderNewPhotos() {
                if (!newPhotos) return;
                newPhotos.innerHTML = '';
            
                newImageFiles.forEach((file, i) => {
                    const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
                    const item = document.createElement('div');
                    item.className = 'photo-item photo-item--new';
                    item.innerHTML = `
                        <img src="${url}" alt="New photo ${i + 1}" />
                        <span class="photo-item__badge">New</span>
                        <button type="button" class="photo-item__remove" data-index="${i}" aria-label="Remove photo">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="12" height="12">
                                <path d="M5 5L15 15M15 5L5 15" stroke-linecap="round" />
                            </svg>
                        </button>
                    `;
                    newPhotos.appendChild(item);
                });
            
                attachNewPhotoEvents();
                updatePhotoCount();
            }
        
            function attachNewPhotoEvents() {
                newPhotos.querySelectorAll('.photo-item__remove').forEach(btn => {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        const index = parseInt(this.dataset.index);
                        newImageFiles.splice(index, 1);
                        renderNewPhotos();
                        updatePhotoInputFiles();
                    });
                });
            }
        
            function updatePhotoInputFiles() {
                const dt = new DataTransfer();
                newImageFiles.forEach(f => dt.items.add(f));
                photoInput.files = dt.files;
            }
        
            function addFiles(files) {
                const remaining = 5 - (existingImageUrls.length + newImageFiles.length);
                const toAdd = Array.from(files).slice(0, remaining);
            
                toAdd.forEach(file => {
                    if (!file.type.match(/^image\/(jpeg|png|webp)$/)) {
                        showToast(file.name + ' is not a supported format.', 'error');
                        return;
                    }
                    if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        showToast(file.name + ' exceeds 5 MB.', 'error');
                        return;
                    }
                    newImageFiles.push(file);
                });
            
                renderNewPhotos();
                updatePhotoInputFiles();
            }
        
            if (existingPhotos) {
                existingPhotos.querySelectorAll('.photo-item__remove').forEach(btn => {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        const item = this.closest('.photo-item');
                        const url = item.dataset.url;
                        removeExistingPhoto(url, item);
                    });
                });
            }
        
            if (photoUploadArea && photoInput) {
                photoUploadArea.addEventListener('click', () => photoInput.click());
                photoUploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); photoUploadArea.classList.add('is-dragging'); });
                photoUploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => photoUploadArea.classList.remove('is-dragging'));
                photoUploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    photoUploadArea.classList.remove('is-dragging');
                    if (e.dataTransfer.files.length) addFiles(e.dataTransfer.files);
                });
            }
        
            if (photoInput) {
                photoInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    if (this.files && this.files.length) addFiles(this.files);
                    this.value = '';
                });
            }
        
            updatePhotoCount();

            // =========================================================
            // FORM SUBMIT
            // =========================================================
        
            const form = document.getElementById('editItemForm');
        
            if (form) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
                    let hasError = false;
                
                    const title = document.getElementById('titleInput')?.value.trim();
                    const price = document.getElementById('priceInput')?.value;
                    const category = document.getElementById('categoryHidden')?.value;
                    const condition = document.getElementById('conditionHidden')?.value;
                    const description = descInput?.value.trim();
                
                    const delivery = document.querySelector('[name="AllowDelivery"]')?.checked;
                    const halfway = document.querySelector('[name="AllowHalfway"]')?.checked;
                    const pickup = document.querySelector('[name="AllowPickup"]')?.checked;
                
                    if (!title) { showToast('Please enter a title.', 'error'); hasError = true; }
                    else if (!price || parseFloat(price) <= 0) { showToast('Please enter a valid price.', 'error'); hasError = true; }
                    else if (!category) { showToast('Please select a category.', 'error'); hasError = true; }
                    else if (!condition) { showToast('Please select the condition.', 'error'); hasError = true; }
                    else if (!description) { showToast('Please enter a description.', 'error'); hasError = true; }
                    else if (!delivery && !halfway && !pickup) { showToast('Please select at least one delivery option.', 'error'); hasError = true; }
                
                    if (hasError) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                    } else {
                        const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
                        if (btn) {
                            btn.disabled = true;
                            btn.querySelector('span').textContent = 'Saving...';
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        
            function showToast(message, type = 'info') {
                const toast = document.createElement('div');
                toast.className = 'app-toast app-toast--' + type;
                toast.textContent = message;
                document.body.appendChild(toast);
                setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 3200);
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

--- Views\Items\Index.cshtml ---
﻿@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.Item>
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "My Listings";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
}

<div class="my-listings">
    <div class="my-listings__header">
        <h1 class="my-listings__title">
            My Listings
            <span class="my-listings__count">@Model.Count item@(Model.Count != 1 ? "s" : "")</span>
        </h1>
        <a asp-action="Create" class="tl-btn tl-btn--primary">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13">
                <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z" />
            </svg>
            List New Item
        </a>
    </div>

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="empty-state">
            <div class="empty-state__icon">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4" width="64" height="64">
                    <rect x="8" y="14" width="48" height="36" rx="6" />
                    <path d="M22 14v-4a6 6 0 0112 0v4" stroke-linecap="round" />
                    <path d="M24 33h16M32 25v16" stroke-linecap="round" />
                </svg>
            </div>
            <h3>No listings yet</h3>
            <p>Start selling by listing your first item!</p>
            <a asp-action="Create" class="tl-btn tl-btn--primary" style="margin-top:1rem">List New Item</a>
        </div>
    }
    else
    {
        <div class="my-listings__grid">
            @foreach (var item in Model)
            {
                var statusClass = item.Status switch
                {
                    ItemStatus.Reserved => "listing-card__status--reserved",
                    ItemStatus.Sold => "listing-card__status--sold",
                    ItemStatus.Disabled => "listing-card__status--disabled",
                    _ => ""
                };
                
                var canDiscount = item.CanBeDiscounted && item.Status == ItemStatus.Available;
                var hasDiscount = item.HasActiveDiscount;

                <div class="listing-card" data-item-id="@item.Id">
                    <div class="listing-card__img-wrap">
                        @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(item.ImageUrl))
                        {
                            <img src="@item.ImageUrl" alt="@item.Title" class="listing-card__img" loading="lazy" />
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="listing-card__img-placeholder">No Image</div>
                        }
                        
                        <span class="listing-card__status @statusClass">@item.Status</span>
                        
                        @if (hasDiscount)
                        {
                            <span class="listing-card__discount-badge">-@(item.DiscountPercentage?.ToString("F0"))%</span>
                        }
                    </div>

                    <div class="listing-card__body">
                        <h3 class="listing-card__title">
                            <a asp-action="Details" asp-route-id="@item.Id">@item.Title</a>
                        </h3>

                        <div class="listing-card__price-section">
                            <span class="listing-card__price">₱@item.Price.ToString("N2")</span>
                            @if (hasDiscount)
                            {
                                <span class="listing-card__original-price">₱@item.OriginalPrice?.ToString("N2")</span>
                                @if (item.DiscountExpiresAt.HasValue)
                                {
                                    var timeLeft = item.DiscountExpiresAt.Value - DateTime.UtcNow;
                                    var expiryText = timeLeft.TotalDays >= 1
                                        ? $"{(int)timeLeft.TotalDays}d left"
                                        : timeLeft.TotalHours >= 1
                                            ? $"{(int)timeLeft.TotalHours}h left"
                                            : "Ending soon";
                                    <div class="listing-card__discount-expiry">⏰ @expiryText</div>
                                }
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="listing-card__meta">
                            <span>@item.Category</span>
                            <span>•</span>
                            <span>@item.Condition</span>
                            @if (item.ListingType == ListingType.Stealable)
                            {
                                <span class="listing-card__type-badge">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10">
                                        <path d="M9.504.43a1.516 1.516 0 012.437 1.713L10.5 6h3.798a1.516 1.516 0 011.149 2.506l-6 7a1.516 1.516 0 01-2.631-1.275L7.5 10H4.701a1.516 1.516 0 01-1.149-2.506l6-7z" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Stealable
                                </span>
                            }
                            @if (hasDiscount)
                            {
                                <span class="has-discount-badge">Discounted</span>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="listing-card__actions">
                            <a asp-action="Edit" asp-route-id="@item.Id" class="listing-card__btn">Edit</a>
                            <a asp-action="Delete" asp-route-id="@item.Id" class="listing-card__btn listing-card__btn--danger">Delete</a>
                            
                            @if (canDiscount && !hasDiscount)
                            {
                                <button type="button" class="listing-card__btn listing-card__btn--discount" data-discount-btn
                                        data-item-id="@item.Id" data-item-title="@item.Title" data-item-price="@item.Price" data-item-image="@item.ImageUrl">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10">
                                        <path d="M14 4.5L9 1.5v6l5-3zM7 2.5L2 5.5v5l5 3 5-3v-5L7 2.5z" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Mark Down
                                </button>
                            }
                            else if (hasDiscount)
                            {
                                <button type="button" class="listing-card__btn" data-remove-discount data-item-id="@item.Id">
                                    Remove Discount
                                </button>
                            }
                            else if (!canDiscount && item.Status == ItemStatus.Available && !hasDiscount)
                            {
                                var hoursUntil = 24 - (int)(DateTime.UtcNow - item.CreatedAt).TotalHours;
                                <button type="button" class="listing-card__btn" disabled title="Discount available in @hoursUntil hour@(hoursUntil != 1 ? "s" : "")">
                                    ⏳ @hoursUntil h
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    }
</div>

@* Discount Modal *@
<div id="discountModal" class="discount-modal-backdrop" style="display:none;">
    <div class="discount-modal">
        <h2 class="discount-modal__title">Apply Discount</h2>

        <div class="discount-modal__item-preview">

--- Views\Orders\Checkout.cshtml ---
﻿@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.CheckoutViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Confirm Purchase";
    Layout = null;

    string condClass = Model.ItemCondition switch
    {
        "New" => "detail-condition--new",
        "Like New" => "detail-condition--like-new",
        "Good" => "detail-condition--good",
        "Fair" => "detail-condition--fair",
        _ => "detail-condition--poor"
    };
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Orders.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="co-shell">

        @* ── Back navigation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <nav class="co-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">
            @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
            {
                <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Shop" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                       class="co-breadcrumb__link">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                    </svg>
                    Back to listing
                </a>
            }
            else
            {
                <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                       class="co-breadcrumb__link">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                    </svg>
                    Back to listing
                </a>
            }
        </nav>

        <header class="co-header">
            <h1 class="co-header__title">
                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Complete Your Steal" : "Confirm Your Purchase")
            </h1>
            <p class="co-header__subtitle">
                @if (Model.WasStolen)
                {
                    @:You stole this item — complete checkout to secure it, or cancel to return it.
                }
                else
                {
                    @:Review the details below before finalising.
                }
            </p>
        </header>

        @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
        {
            <div class="co-alert co-alert--error" role="alert">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-8-5a.75.75 0 01.75.75v4.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-4.5A.75.75 0 0110 5zm0 10a1 1 0 100-2 1 1 0 000 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
                @errMsg
                @if (errMsg.Contains("wallet") || errMsg.Contains("balance"))
                {
                    <a asp-action="AddFunds" asp-controller="Wallet" class="co-alert__link">Add funds →</a>
                }
            </div>
        }

        <div class="co-grid">

            @* ════════════ LEFT — Item summary ════════════ *@
            <div class="co-summary-col">

                <div class="co-item-card">
                    <div class="co-item-card__img-wrap">
                        @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.ItemImageUrl))
                        {
                            <img src="@Model.ItemImageUrl" alt="Photo of @Model.ItemTitle"
                                 class="co-item-card__img" loading="eager" />
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="co-item-card__img co-item-card__img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                    <rect x="6" y="10" width="52" height="44" rx="6" />
                                    <circle cx="22" cy="26" r="6" />
                                    <path d="M6 46l16-14 10 10 8-7 18 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                </svg>
                            </div>
                        }
                        @if (Model.IsStealable)
                        {
                            <span class="co-item-card__stealable-badge">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M7.75 1.5L2.5 8h4.25L5.5 12.5 11.5 6H7.25L7.75 1.5z" />
                                </svg>
                                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Stolen" : "Stealable")
                            </span>
                        }
                    </div>

                    <div class="co-item-card__body">
                        <div class="co-item-card__meta">
                            <span class="co-item-card__category">@Model.ItemCategory</span>
                            <span class="co-item-card__condition @condClass">@Model.ItemCondition</span>

                            @* P2P: show item size if available *@
                            @if (!Model.IsShopOrder && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.ItemSize))
                            {
                                <span class="co-item-card__size">@Model.ItemSize</span>
                            }

                            @* Shop (Option B): show variant, size, and quantity chips *@
                            @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                            {
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.SelectedVariantName) && Model.SelectedVariantName != "Default")
                                {
                                    <span class="co-item-card__size co-chip--shop">@Model.SelectedVariantName</span>
                                }
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.SelectedSize))
                                {
                                    <span class="co-item-card__size co-chip--shop">@Model.SelectedSize</span>
                                }
                                <span class="co-item-card__size co-chip--qty">×@Model.Quantity</span>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <h2 class="co-item-card__title">@Model.ItemTitle</h2>

                        <div class="co-item-card__seller">
                            <div class="co-item-card__seller-avatar" aria-hidden="true">
                                @char.ToUpper(Model.SellerName.FirstOrDefault())
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <p class="co-item-card__seller-label">Sold by</p>
                                <p class="co-item-card__seller-name">@Model.SellerName</p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                @* ── Left-column notices ──────────────────────────────────────── *@
                @if (Model.WasStolen)
                {
                    <div class="co-cancel-steal-notice" role="note">

                                                <path d="M12 2a7 7 0 00-7 7c0 5 7 13 7 13s7-8 7-13a7 7 0 00-7-7z" />
                                                <circle cx="12" cy="9" r="3" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__info">

                            }

                            @if (Model.AllowPickup)
                            {
                                <label class="co-fulfillment-option @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Pickup" ? "co-fulfillment-option--selected" : "")" data-method="Pickup">
                                    <input type="radio" name="fulfillmentMethod" value="Pickup" class="co-fulfillment-radio"
                                    @(Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod == "Pickup" ? "checked" : "") />
                                    <div class="co-fulfillment-option__content">
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__icon">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="24" height="24">
                                                <path d="M3 9l9-7 9 7v11a2 2 0 01-2 2H5a2 2 0 01-2-2V9z" />
                                                <path d="M9 22V12h6v10" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="co-fulfillment-option__info">
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__title">Self Pickup</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__price">No delivery fee</span>
                                            <span class="co-fulfillment-option__description">Pick up directly from the seller. A chat will open after checkout to arrange details.</span>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </label>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Payment method selector ──────────────────────────────── *@
                    <div class="co-pay-section">
                        <h3 class="co-pay-section__heading">Payment method</h3>

                        <div class="co-pay-options" id="payOptions">

                            @* Wallet option *@
                            <label class="co-pay-option @(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "" : "co-pay-option--disabled")"
                                   id="payWalletLabel">
                                <input type="radio"
                                       name="paymentMethod"
                                       value="Wallet"
                                       class="co-pay-radio"
                                       id="payWallet"
                                @(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "checked" : "disabled") />
                                <div class="co-pay-option__icon">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path d="M1 4.25a3.733 3.733 0 012-.575h13.5c.43 0 .845.069 1.232.198A2.25 2.25 0 0015.5 3h-11a3 3 0 00-3 3v1.25H1V4.25zM3.75 7A.75.75 0 013 6.25v-.5A2.75 2.75 0 015.75 3h8.5A2.75 2.75 0 0117 5.75v.5a.75.75 0 01-.75.75h-12.5z" />
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 8.5v6A2.5 2.5 0 003.5 17h13a2.5 2.5 0 002.5-2.5v-6A2.5 2.5 0 0016.5 6h-13A2.5 2.5 0 001 8.5zm14.5 3a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <div class="co-pay-option__body">
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__name">ThriftLoop Wallet</p>
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__detail">
                                        Balance: <strong>₱@Model.BuyerBalance.ToString("N2")</strong>
                                        @if (!Model.HasSufficientBalance)
                                        {
                                            <span class="co-pay-option__insufficient">
                                                — insufficient
                                                (<a asp-action="AddFunds" asp-controller="Wallet">add funds</a>)
                                            </span>
                                        }
                                        else
                                        {
                                            <text> · funds held in escrow until delivery</text>
                                        }
                                    </p>
                                </div>
                            </label>

                            @* Cash on Delivery option *@
                            <label class="co-pay-option" id="payCodLabel">
                                <input type="radio"
                                       name="paymentMethod"
                                       value="Cash"
                                       class="co-pay-radio"
                                       id="payCod"
                                @(!Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "checked" : "") />
                                <div class="co-pay-option__icon">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zM8.798 7.45c.512-.67 1.135-.95 1.702-.95s1.19.28 1.702.95a.75.75 0 001.192-.91C12.637 5.55 11.596 5 10.5 5s-2.137.55-2.894 1.54A4.501 4.501 0 007 9.5c0 1.079.37 2.077 1 2.879V14a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-1.734c-.35-.588-.5-1.14-.5-1.766 0-.863.275-1.61.798-2.05zM10 14.25a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <div class="co-pay-option__body">
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__name">Cash on Delivery / Meetup</p>
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__detail" id="cashPaymentDetail">Pay cash when your item arrives</p>
                                </div>
                            </label>

                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Confirm form: routes to the right action based on order type ── *@
                    @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                    {
                        <form asp-action="ConfirmShopOrder" asp-controller="Orders"
                              method="post" id="confirmForm">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <input type="hidden" name="skuId" value="@Model.SkuId" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="quantity" value="@Model.Quantity" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="paymentMethod" id="paymentMethodInput"
                                   value="@(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "Wallet" : "Cash")" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="fulfillmentMethod" id="fulfillmentMethodInput"
                                   value="@Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod" />

                            <button type="submit" class="co-confirm-btn" id="confirmBtn">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                Confirm Purchase
                            </button>
                        </form>

                        <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Shop" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                               class="co-cancel-link">
                            Cancel and go back
                        </a>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <form asp-action="ConfirmOrder" asp-controller="Orders"
                              method="post" id="confirmForm">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <input type="hidden" name="itemId" value="@Model.ItemId" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="paymentMethod" id="paymentMethodInput"
                                   value="@(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "Wallet" : "Cash")" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="fulfillmentMethod" id="fulfillmentMethodInput"
                                   value="@Model.SelectedFulfillmentMethod" />

                            <button type="submit" class="co-confirm-btn" id="confirmBtn">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Confirm Steal Purchase" : "Confirm Purchase")
                            </button>
                        </form>

                        @if (!Model.WasStolen)
                        {
                            <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                                   class="co-cancel-link">
                                Cancel and go back
                            </a>
                        }
                    }

                </div>

            </div>

        </div>

    </div>

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';

                var paymentRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.co-pay-radio');
                var paymentHiddenInput = document.getElementById('paymentMethodInput');
                var fulfillmentRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.co-fulfillment-radio');
                var fulfillmentHiddenInput = document.getElementById('fulfillmentMethodInput');
                var form = document.getElementById('confirmForm');
                var btn = document.getElementById('confirmBtn');
                var deliveryFeeRow = document.getElementById('deliveryFeeRow');
                var deliveryFeeValue = document.getElementById('deliveryFeeValue');
                var finalPriceDisplay = document.getElementById('finalPriceDisplay');
                var cashPaymentDetail = document.getElementById('cashPaymentDetail');
                var fulfillmentOptions = document.querySelectorAll('.co-fulfillment-option');

                var basePrice = @Model.BasePrice;
                var stealPremium = @(Model.WasStolen? Model.StealPremium: 0);
                var deliveryFee = @Model.DeliveryFee;
                var quantity = @Model.Quantity;

                // Function to update UI based on selected fulfillment method
                function updateFulfillmentUI(method) {
                    var isDelivery = method === 'Delivery';
                
                    // Update option selection styling
                    fulfillmentOptions.forEach(function(opt) {
                        opt.classList.remove('co-fulfillment-option--selected');
                    });
                    var selectedOption = document.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-option[data-method="' + method + '"]');
                    if (selectedOption) {
                        selectedOption.classList.add('co-fulfillment-option--selected');
                    }
                
                    // Show/hide delivery fee row
                    if (deliveryFeeRow) {
                        deliveryFeeRow.style.display = isDelivery ? 'flex' : 'none';
                    }
                
                    // Calculate and update final price
                    var itemTotal = basePrice + stealPremium;
                    var finalPrice = isDelivery ? itemTotal + deliveryFee : itemTotal;
                
                    if (finalPriceDisplay) {
                        finalPriceDisplay.textContent = '₱' + finalPrice.toFixed(2).replace(/\d(?=(\d{3})+\.)/g, '$&,');
                    }
                
                    // Update cash payment detail text
                    if (cashPaymentDetail) {
                        if (isDelivery) {
                            cashPaymentDetail.textContent = 'Pay cash to the rider upon delivery';
                        } else if (method === 'Halfway') {
                            cashPaymentDetail.textContent = 'Pay cash to the seller when you meet';
                        } else if (method === 'Pickup') {
                            cashPaymentDetail.textContent = 'Pay cash to the seller when you pick up the item';
                        }
                    }
                
                    // Update hidden input
                    if (fulfillmentHiddenInput) {
                        fulfillmentHiddenInput.value = method;
                    }
                }

                // Keep payment method input in sync
                paymentRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                    radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                        if (paymentHiddenInput) paymentHiddenInput.value = radio.value;
                    });
                });

                // Handle fulfillment method selection
                fulfillmentRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                    radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                        updateFulfillmentUI(radio.value);
                    });
                });

                // Also handle click on the whole option card
                fulfillmentOptions.forEach(function(opt) {
                    opt.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        var radio = this.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-radio');
                        if (radio && !radio.disabled) {
                            radio.checked = true;
                            updateFulfillmentUI(radio.value);
                        }
                    });
                });

                // Initialize UI with default selection
                var checkedFulfillment = document.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-radio:checked');
                if (checkedFulfillment) {
                    updateFulfillmentUI(checkedFulfillment.value);
                } else {
                    // Default to first available option
                    var firstOption = document.querySelector('.co-fulfillment-radio');
                    if (firstOption) {
                        firstOption.checked = true;
                        updateFulfillmentUI(firstOption.value);
                    }
                }

                // Disable button + show spinner on submit
                if (form && btn) {
                    form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                        btn.disabled = true;
                        btn.innerHTML =
                            '<svg class="co-spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" ' +
                            'width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">' +
                            '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".3"/>' +
                            '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 017 7h-1.5A5.5 5.5 0 0010 4.5V3z"/>' +
                            '</svg> Confirming\u2026';
                    });
                }

            }());
    </script>

    <style>
            /* Fulfillment Section Styles */
            .co-fulfillment-section {
                margin-top: 1.5rem;
                padding-top: 1rem;
                border-top: 1px solid var(--co-border, #e4e4ea);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-section__heading {
                font-size: 1rem;
                font-weight: 600;
                margin-bottom: 1rem;
                color: var(--co-text, #111827);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-options {
                display: flex;
                flex-direction: column;
                gap: 0.75rem;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option {
                cursor: pointer;
                display: block;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-radio {
                display: none;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__content {
                display: flex;
                align-items: flex-start;
                gap: 1rem;
                padding: 1rem;
                border: 1.5px solid var(--co-border, #e4e4ea);
                border-radius: 12px;
                transition: all 0.15s;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option--selected .co-fulfillment-option__content,
            .co-fulfillment-radio:checked + .co-fulfillment-option__content {
                border-color: var(--co-primary, #2d1b69);
                background: rgba(45, 27, 105, 0.02);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__icon {
                flex-shrink: 0;
                color: #6b7280;
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option--selected .co-fulfillment-option__icon,
            .co-fulfillment-radio:checked + .co-fulfillment-option__content .co-fulfillment-option__icon {
                color: var(--co-primary, #2d1b69);
            }

            .co-fulfillment-option__info {
                flex: 1;
            }

                        <path d="M1 4.25a3.733 3.733 0 012-.575h13.5c.43 0 .845.069 1.232.198A2.25 2.25 0 0015.5 3h-11a3 3 0 00-3 3v1.25H1V4.25z" />
                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 8.5v6A2.5 2.5 0 003.5 17h13a2.5 2.5 0 002.5-2.5v-6A2.5 2.5 0 0016.5 6h-13A2.5 2.5 0 001 8.5zm14.5 3a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />

                    My Wallet

                <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--ghost mp-header__cta">
                    Browse listings
                </a>
            </div>
        </header>

        @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] is string successMsg)

                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">

                </svg>
                @successMsg
            </div>
        }
        @if (TempData["InfoMessage"] is string infoMsg)
        {
            <div class="mp-toast mp-toast--info" id="mpToast" role="status">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a.75.75 0 000 1.5h.253a.25.25 0 01.244.304l-.459 2.066A1.75 1.75 0 0010.747 15H11a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-.253a.25.25 0 01-.244-.304l.459-2.066A1.75 1.75 0 009.253 9H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
                @infoMsg
            </div>
        }
        @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
        {
            <div class="mp-toast mp-toast--error" id="mpToast" role="alert">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">

                </svg>
                @errMsg
            </div>
        }

        @if (!Model.Any())

        else
        {
            <div class="mp-list">
                @foreach (var order in Model)
                {
                    var sellerEmail = order.Seller?.Email ?? string.Empty;
                    var sellerDisplay = sellerEmail.Contains('@') ? sellerEmail.Split('@')[0] : sellerEmail;

                    string statusClass = order.Status switch
                    {
                        OrderStatus.Pending => "mp-status--pending",
                        OrderStatus.Completed => "mp-status--completed",
                        OrderStatus.Cancelled => "mp-status--cancelled",
                        _ => ""
                    };

                    string statusLabel = order.Status switch
                    {
                        OrderStatus.Pending => "Pending",
                        OrderStatus.Completed => "Completed",
                        OrderStatus.Cancelled => "Cancelled",
                        _ => order.Status.ToString()
                    };

                    string payLabel = order.PaymentMethod switch
                    {
                        PaymentMethod.Wallet => "Wallet (escrow)",
                        PaymentMethod.Cash => "Cash on Delivery",
                        _ => order.PaymentMethod.ToString()
                    };

                    // Check delivery status to determine if buyer can confirm receipt
                    bool canMarkDelivered = order.Status == OrderStatus.Pending
                        && order.Delivery != null
                        && order.Delivery.Status == DeliveryStatus.Delivered;
                    
                    // Show delivery status message
                    string deliveryStatusMessage = order.Delivery?.Status switch
                    {
                        DeliveryStatus.Available => "Waiting for a rider to accept this delivery.",
                        DeliveryStatus.Accepted => "A rider has accepted your delivery and is on the way to pick up the item.",
                        DeliveryStatus.PickedUp => "Rider has picked up your item and is en route.",
                        DeliveryStatus.Delivered => "Rider has delivered your item. Please confirm receipt.",
                        DeliveryStatus.Completed => "Delivery completed. Thank you!",
                        _ => "Delivery pending."
                    };

                    <article class="mp-row">

                        <div class="mp-row__img-wrap">
                            @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(order.Item?.ImageUrl))
                            {
                                <img src="@order.Item.ImageUrl" alt="@order.Item?.Title"
                                     class="mp-row__img" loading="lazy" />
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <div class="mp-row__img mp-row__img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                        <rect x="3" y="5" width="26" height="22" rx="3" />
                                        <circle cx="11" cy="13" r="3" />
                                        <path d="M3 23l8-7 5 5 4-3 9 7" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="mp-row__body">
                            <div class="mp-row__top">
                                <h3 class="mp-row__title">
                                    @(order.Item?.Title ?? "Item #" + order.ItemId)
                                </h3>
                                <span class="mp-status @statusClass">@statusLabel</span>
                            </div>

                            <p class="mp-row__seller">Seller: @sellerDisplay</p>

                            @* Payment method pill *@
                            <p class="mp-row__pay">
                                <span class="mp-pay-pill mp-pay-pill--@(order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet ? "wallet" : "cod")">
                                    @if (order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet)
                                    {
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 3.5A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 2h9A1.5 1.5 0 0113 3.5v7A1.5 1.5 0 0111.5 12h-9A1.5 1.5 0 011 10.5v-7zm10.5 2.5a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path d="M7 1a6 6 0 100 12A6 6 0 007 1zm.6 8.9H6.4V6.4h1.2v3.5zm0-4.6H6.4V4.1h1.2v1.2z" />
                                        </svg>
                                    }
                                    @payLabel
                                </span>
                            </p>

                            @* Delivery status message *@
                            @if (order.Delivery != null)
                            {
                                <p class="mp-row__delivery" style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: #6b7280; margin: 0.5rem 0;">
                                    📦 @deliveryStatusMessage
                                </p>
                            }

                                Ordered

                                    @order.OrderDate.ToString("MMMM d, yyyy · h:mm tt") UTC
                                </time>
                            </p>

                            @* Mark Delivered — only visible when delivery is in Delivered state *@
                            @if (canMarkDelivered)
                            {
                                <form asp-action="MarkDelivered"
                                      asp-controller="Orders"
                                      asp-route-orderId="@order.Id"
                                      method="post"
                                      class="mp-deliver-form"
                                      onsubmit="return confirm('Confirm receipt of this order? This will release payment to the seller.');">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <button type="submit" class="mp-deliver-btn">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                        I have received this item
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="mp-row__price-col">
                            <span class="mp-row__price">₱@order.FinalPrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                            <span class="mp-row__price-label">Final price</span>
                        </div>

                    </article>
                }
            </div>
        }

    </div>

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';
                var toast = document.getElementById('mpToast');
                if (toast) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        toast.style.opacity = '0';
                        setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                    }, 5000);
                }
            }());
    </script>
</body>
