--- Views\Shared\_Navbar.cshtml ---
@using System.Security.Claims
@using ThriftLoop.Repositories.Interface
@using ThriftLoop.Services.Interface
@inject IShopRepository ShopRepo
@inject ICartRepository CartRepo
@inject IItemLikeRepository LikeRepo
@inject IChatService ChatService

@{
    var userEmail = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.Email)?.Value
                        ?? User.Identity?.Name
                        ?? string.Empty;
    var displayName = userEmail.Contains('@') ? userEmail.Split('@')[0] : userEmail;
    var currentPath = Context.Request.Path.Value ?? string.Empty;

    // Check if current user is a Rider
    var isRider = User.HasClaim(c => c.Type == "IsRider" && c.Value == "true");

    // Resolve live shop name for the navbar pill (only for Sellers)
    var shopLabel = "My Shop";

    // Get cart count, likes count, and unread message count for authenticated users
    int cartCount = 0;
    int likesCount = 0;
    int unreadMessageCount = 0;

    var rawId = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier)?.Value;
    if (int.TryParse(rawId, out var navUserId))
    {
        if (!isRider && User.IsInRole("Seller"))
        {
            var shop = await ShopRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop?.ShopName))
                shopLabel = shop.ShopName;
        }

        if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && !isRider)
        {
            cartCount = await CartRepo.GetCountByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            var likes = await LikeRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            likesCount = likes.Count;
            unreadMessageCount = await ChatService.GetTotalUnreadCountAsync(navUserId);
        }
    }
}

<nav class="tl-nav">
    <div class="tl-nav__inner">

        @* Logo - Redirects based on user type *@
        @if (isRider)
        {
            <a asp-controller="Rider" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">ThriftLoop Rider</a>
        }
        else
        {
            <a asp-controller="Home" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">ThriftLoop</a>
        }

        @* Centre navigation - Hide for Riders *@
        @if (!isRider)
        {
            <ul class="tl-nav__links" role="list">
                <li>
                    <a asp-controller="Home"
                           asp-action="Index"
                           class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath == "/" || currentPath.StartsWith("/Home", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                        For You
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li class="tl-nav__divider" aria-hidden="true"></li>
                <li>
                    <a asp-controller="Sellers"
                           asp-action="Index"
                           class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Sellers", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                        Sellers
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li class="tl-nav__divider" aria-hidden="true"></li>
                <li>
                    <a asp-controller="Items"
                           asp-action="Index"
                           class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Items", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                        My Listings
                    </a>
                </li>
            </ul>
        }

        @* ── Right side: My Shop pill + user dropdown ────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="tl-nav__user">
            @if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true)
            {
                @* My Shop pill — only for Sellers (not riders, not admins) *@
                @if (!isRider && User.IsInRole("Seller"))
                {
                    <a asp-controller="Shop"
                           asp-action="Mine"
                           class="tl-nav__shop-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Shop", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__shop-btn--active" : "")">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8 1a2.5 2.5 0 00-2.5 2.5H3.5A1.5 1.5 0 002 5v8.5A1.5 1.5 0 003.5 15h9a1.5 1.5 0 001.5-1.5V5a1.5 1.5 0 00-1.5-1.5h-2A2.5 2.5 0 008 1zm0 1.5A1 1 0 019 3.5v0H7v0A1 1 0 018 2.5zm-2.5 2H4a.5.5 0 00-.5.5v8a.5.5 0 00.5.5h8a.5.5 0 00.5-.5V5a.5.5 0 00-.5-.5h-1.5v.75a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V4.5h-2v.75a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V4.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        @shopLabel
                    </a>
                }

                @* Messages icon — for all authenticated non-rider users *@
                @if (!isRider)
                {
                    <a asp-controller="Chat" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__icon-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Chat", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__icon-btn--active" : "")" title="Messages">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M21 15a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H7l-4 4V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h14a2 2 0 0 1 2 2z" />
                        </svg>
                        @if (unreadMessageCount > 0)
                        {
                            <span class="tl-nav__badge message-badge" id="chatUnreadBadge">@(unreadMessageCount > 99 ? "99+" : unreadMessageCount.ToString())</span>
                        }
                    </a>

                    @* Cart icon — for all authenticated non-rider users *@
                    <a asp-controller="Cart" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__icon-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Cart", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__icon-btn--active" : "")" title="Shopping Cart">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M3 3h2l.4 2M7 13h10l4-8H5.4M7 13L5.4 5M7 13l-2.293 2.293c-.63.63-.184 1.707.707 1.707H17m0 0a2 2 0 1 0 0 4 2 2 0 0 0 0-4zm-8 2a2 2 0 1 1 0 4 2 2 0 0 1 0-4z" />
                        </svg>
                        @if (cartCount > 0)
                        {
                            <span class="tl-nav__badge cart-badge">@cartCount</span>
                        }
                    </a>

                    @* Likes icon *@
                    <a asp-controller="Likes" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__icon-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Likes", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__icon-btn--active" : "")" title="Liked Items">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M20.84 4.61a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 0L12 5.67l-1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 7.78l1.06 1.06L12 21.23l7.78-7.78 1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 000-7.78z" />
                        </svg>
                        @if (likesCount > 0)
                        {
                            <span class="tl-nav__badge likes-badge">@likesCount</span>
                        }
                    </a>
                }

                @* User dropdown *@
                <div class="tl-nav__dropdown">
                    <button class="tl-nav__dropdown-toggle" id="userDropdown" aria-expanded="false">

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const dropdownToggle = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
        const dropdownMenu = document.getElementById('userDropdownMenu');

        if (dropdownToggle && dropdownMenu) {
            dropdownToggle.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const isExpanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', !isExpanded);
                dropdownMenu.classList.toggle('show');
            });

            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!dropdownToggle.contains(e.target) && !dropdownMenu.contains(e.target)) {
                    dropdownToggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    dropdownMenu.classList.remove('show');
                }
            });
        }

        // Poll for unread message count updates
        function updateUnreadCount() {
            fetch('/Chat/UnreadCount')
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    const badge = document.getElementById('chatUnreadBadge');
                    if (badge) {
                        if (data.unreadCount > 0) {
                            badge.textContent = data.unreadCount > 99 ? '99+' : data.unreadCount;
                            badge.style.display = 'flex';
                        } else {
                            badge.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }
                })
                .catch(() => {});
        }

        // Only poll if user is authenticated and not a rider
        @if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && !isRider)
        {
                <text>
                    setInterval(updateUnreadCount, 30000); // Poll every 30 seconds
                </text>
        }
    });
</script>

    var storeAddrError = ViewData.ModelState.ContainsKey("StoreAddress")
                         && ViewData.ModelState["StoreAddress"]!.Errors.Count > 0;
    var storeAddrErrorMsg = storeAddrError
                            ? ViewData.ModelState["StoreAddress"]!.Errors[0].ErrorMessage
                            : string.Empty;
}

            font-family: 'DM Serif Display', serif;
            font-size: 1.5rem;
            color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
            background: transparent;
            width: 100%;
        }

        .addfunds-quick {
            display: flex;
            gap: 0.5rem;
            justify-content: center;
            flex-wrap: wrap;
        }

        .addfunds-quick__btn {
            padding: 0.4rem 0.875rem;
            border: 1.5px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
            border-radius: 6px;
            background: #fff;
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.875rem;
            font-weight: 500;
            color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
            cursor: pointer;
            transition: border-color 0.15s, background 0.15s;
        }

            .addfunds-quick__btn:hover,
            .addfunds-quick__btn--active {
                border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
                background: color-mix(in srgb, var(--color-primary, #2d5a27) 6%, transparent);
                color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            }

        .addfunds-submit {
            width: 100%;
            justify-content: center;
        }

        .addfunds-methods {
            margin-top: 2rem;
        }

        .addfunds-methods__label {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.78rem;
            color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
            text-transform: uppercase;
            letter-spacing: 0.05em;
            margin: 0 0 0.625rem;
        }

        .addfunds-methods__logos {
            display: flex;
            gap: 0.5rem;
            justify-content: center;
            flex-wrap: wrap;
        }

        .addfunds-method-pill {
            padding: 0.3rem 0.75rem;
            border: 1px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
            border-radius: 99px;
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.78rem;
            color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
            opacity: 0.65;
        }
    </style>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var input   = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var form    = document.getElementById('addFundsForm');
            var btn     = document.getElementById('addFundsBtn');
            var presets = document.querySelectorAll('.addfunds-quick__btn');

            presets.forEach(function (p) {
                p.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    if (!input) return;
                    input.value = p.dataset.amount;
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    p.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                });
            });

            if (input) {
                input.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    presets.forEach(function (b) {
                        if (b.dataset.amount === input.value) b.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                    });
                });
            }

            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'Processing…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

                <div class="wlt-tx-list">
                    @foreach (var tx in Model.RecentTransactions)
                    {
                        // Determine if this transaction is a credit (money coming IN to the current user/rider)
                        bool isCredit;
                        
                        if (isRider)
                        {
                            // For riders: credit if ToRiderId matches current user
                            isCredit = tx.ToRiderId == Model.CurrentUserId
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            // For regular users: credit if ToUserId matches current user
                            isCredit = tx.ToUserId == Model.CurrentUserId
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        }
                        
                        bool isDebit = !isCredit;

                        string typeLabel = tx.Type switch
                        {
                            TransactionType.EscrowHold => "Escrow Hold",
                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "Escrow Release",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "Withdrawal",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "Cash Collected",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "Funds Added",
                            TransactionType.DeliveryFeePayment => "Delivery Fee",

                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "unlock",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "arrow-up",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "cash",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "plus",
                            TransactionType.DeliveryFeePayment => "delivery",
                            _ => "dot"
                        };

                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "unlock")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M14.5 1A4.5 4.5 0 0010 5.5V9H3a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-1.5V5.5a3 3 0 116 0v2.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0014.5 1z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var amountInput = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var allBtn      = document.getElementById('withdrawAllBtn');
            var wdForm      = document.getElementById('wdForm');
            var wdSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('wdSubmitBtn');
            var methodRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-radio');
            var methodLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-option');

            // "Withdraw all" shortcut
            if (allBtn && amountInput) {
                allBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    amountInput.value = amountInput.max;
                });
            }

            // Sync method option visual state with radio selection
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio, i) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    methodLabels.forEach(function (lbl) { lbl.classList.remove('wd-method-option--active'); });
                    if (radio.checked) methodLabels[i].classList.add('wd-method-option--active');
                });
            });

            // Update reference hint based on method
            var referenceHint = document.getElementById('referenceHint');
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (!referenceHint) return;
                    referenceHint.textContent = radio.value === '1'
                        ? 'Your preferred pickup location or reference code.'
                        : 'Your bank account number or preferred pickup reference.';
                });
            });

            // Disable submit while in-flight
            if (wdForm && wdSubmitBtn) {
                wdForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    wdSubmitBtn.disabled = true;
                    wdSubmitBtn.textContent = 'Submitting…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}
